[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue, italicized font. The formula is:
`scalerChannelType = decimatescalingFactor · prachtTimeAgcGain · prchScalingFactor · 2^-(IQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.5.2-2)

For short format in HST scenario

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light gray, italicized font against a white background. The formula is presented on two lines.
The first line reads: `scaler ChannelType`
The second line starts with an equals sign and continues with a multiplication expression:
`= decimateScaling Factor · prachTimeAgcGain · fdAgcGain`
Below this, there is another term, likely part of the same expression, starting with a dot:
`· prchScaling Factor · 2-(Q1Q-in)`
The formula appears to define a variable `scaler ChannelType` as a product of several factors: `decimateScaling Factor`, `prachTimeAgcGain`, `fdAgcGain`, `prchScaling Factor`, and a power of 2 term `2-(Q1Q-in)`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]     (equation 2.5.5.2-3)

For eCPRI case:

For traffic channel type

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font against a white background. The equation is:
`scalerChannelType = 2^nShift . 2^-(IQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]    (equation 2.5.5.2-4)

For PRACH

[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue font on a white background. The formula is:
`scalerChannelType = 2^nShift · prchScalingFactor · 2^-(IQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]    (equation 2.5.5.2-5)

**For short format in HST scenario and For FDD eCPRI**

[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue, italicized font. The equation is:
`scalerChannelType = 2^nshift · fdAgeGain · prchScalingFactor · 2^-(qIQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]    (equation 2.5.5.2-6)

Then

[image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`scalerChannelType_dB = 20 * log10(scalerChannelType)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]    (equation 2.5.5.2-7)

For the CPRI case and OBSAI case, rxScalingFactor represents average time domain power over the I and Q samples of an OFDM symbol with respect to the system full bandwidth, as stated in CPRI IDT requirements in section [11415902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-R1IfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), the rxScalingFactor is calculated with sampling rate of the respective bandwidth group in samples/s, converting it to OFDM symbol level, then it is corresponding to FFT size. And those power measurements are calculated with average on one sub carrier and normalized to one PRB (12 sub carriers for traffic channel) excluding PRACH taking band width ratio into calculation separately. So, for traffic channel, regarding time domain to freqency domain conversion taking FFT size into account (including fftScalingFactor = 1 since normalized FFT is utilized) to get power unit,

[image-7][image\_desc]powerUnitChannelType$*{dBm}$ = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - 10 log$*{10}$(N$*{FFT}$) - scalerChannelType$*{dB}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]    (equation 2.5.5.2-8)

where, [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, partial view of text. The visible text appears to be "NFFT". The letters are in a light blue color with a slight gradient and a subtle shadow effect. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8] is the FFT size per normal bandwidth without split.

(For example: if 40MHz with 61.44Msps is split to 2x20MHz with 30.72Msps, then NFFT = 4096 for power calculation. The split carrier part  impact shall be compensated by rxScalingFactor referring to section [11418606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-Zw-fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for implementation simplicity.)

**Note:  only ABIO supports split mode.**

For the eCPRI case, rxScalingFactor represents average frequency domain power over the I and Q samples of an OFDM symbol with respect to the bandwidth of one sub carrier, so the power unit shall be

[image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a single line of text. The text is in a light gray color against a white background. The text reads: "powerUnitChannelType\_dBm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - scalerChannelType\_dB".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3143.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]    (equation 2.5.5.2-9)

Above requirement support based on technology and HW board as below table:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Technology** | **Loki** | **UL channels & Signals** |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI | supported | PUSCH/DMRS, PUCCH/DMRS, SRS, PRACH |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | supported | PUSCH/DMRS, PUCCH/DMRS, SRS, PRACH |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | PUSCH/DMRS, PUCCH/DMRS, SRS, PRACH |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | supported | PUSCH/DMRS, PUCCH/DMRS, SRS, **[CB010315-SR-A]** RIM-RS, **[End CB010315-SR-A]** PRACH |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | PUSCH/DMRS, PUCCH/DMRS, SRS, RIM-RS, PRACH |
| FR2-TDD-CPRI | - | - |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | PUSCH/DMRS, PUCCH/DMRS, SRS |

RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2.

The multiplication is indicated by a dot (`.`).[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3149.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]    (equation 2.5.5.3-1)

For PRACH:

For CPRI case and OBSAI case

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue, italicized font against a white background. The formula is:
`scaler Channel Type = decimateScaling Factor * sqrt(N_IFFT) * fdAgcGain * prchScaling Factor * 2^-(Q_IQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3149.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] (equation 2.5.5.3-2)

For eCPRI case

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a single line of text with a mathematical formula. The text is in a dark blue color against a white background. The formula reads:
`scalerChannelType = fdAgeGain · prchScalingFactor · 2^-(IQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3149.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]    (equation 2.5.5.3-3)

Then

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`scalerChannelType_dB = 20 * log10(scalerChannelType)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3149.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]    (equation 2.5.5.3-4)

For the CPRI case and OBSAI case, rxScalingFactor represents average time domain power over the I and Q samples of an OFDM symbol with respect to the system full bandwidth, as stated in CPRI IDT requirements in section [11415902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-R1IfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), the rxScalingFactor is calculated with sampling rate of the respective bandwidth group in samples/s, converting it to OFDM symbol level, then it is corresponding to FFT size. And those power measurements are calculated with average on one sub carrier and normalized to one PRB (12 sub carriers for traffic channel) excluding PRACH, which takes band width ratio into calculation separately. So, for traffic channel, regarding time domain to frequency domain conversion taking FFT size into account  to get power unit (**here combining fftScalingFactor due to un-normalized FFT, however, L1SW can perform fftScalingFactor separately in linear power calculation, it depends on SW design's convenience and efficiency and in that case, -20log10(N**FFT**) in below equation shall be replaced by -10log10(N**FFT**) in case of fftScalingFactor to be compensated in ScalerChannelType),*****\****\*

[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue font on a white background. The formula reads: "powerUnitChannelTypedsm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - 20 log10(NFFT) - scaler ChannelTypeds".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3149.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]    (equation 2.5.5.3-5)

For the eCPRI case, rxScalingFactor represents average frequency domain power over the I and Q samples of an OFDM symbol with respect to the bandwidth of one sub carrier, so the power unit shall be

[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a single line of text. The text is in a light gray color against a white background. The text reads: "powerUnitChannelType\_dBm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - scalerChannelType\_dB".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3149.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]    (equation 2.5.5.3-6)

## 2.5.6 Introduction of provisional corrective terms

### 2.5.6.1 For Loner only

**2.5.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `11420257`)

For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
11420257:
For Loner only
To account for the possibility that the formulas in the previous sub-sections, allowing the conversion of measurements to dBm before they are sent to 5G-L2-PS, are incorrect due to some gains being overlooked in the Rx processing chain, it is proposed, at least in the short term, to introduce additive corrective terms (in dB) in the previous power computation formulas. The assumptions with these corrective terms is that the previous formulas are wrong only due to the omission of a fixed gain. Assuming that this overlooked gain can be different for each physical signal or channel, a corrective term is proposed for each physical signal and channel. Note that it is not certain a priori that the corrective term should be the same for all power measurements performed on a particular physical signal or channel, but it is considered a reasonable assumption. It is hoped that measurements will be made soon that will allow to confirm this assumption.

The corrective terms would be determined by calibration (i.e., by comparing measured and trusted values of signal or noise powers with the values computed by L1-SW and by compensating any difference by corrective terms).

The corrective terms will be denoted pCorChannelType (pCorPusch, pCorPucch (F0/F1/F2/F3), pCorSrs and pCorPrach for PUSCH, PUCCH (F0/F1/F2/F3), SRS and PRACH, respectively) and will be expressed in dB.  The formulas including the corrective terms are of the type:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
$A\_{dBm} = 10 \cdot \log\_{10} A + \text{powerUnitChannelType}\_{dBm} + \text{pCorChannelType}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3157.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]    (equation 2.5.6.1-1)

and

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
$B\_{dBm} = 10 \cdot \log\_{10} B + \text{powerUnitChannelType}\_{dBm} + \text{pCorChannelType}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3157.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.6.1-2)

The default value for all pCorChannelType parameters will be 0, since the formulas in section [11419826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-epfvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) are believed to be correct, but this may evolve depending on the outcome of the calibrations.

The intention is that all there corrective terms are eventually removed once confirmation has been obtained through measurements that all power computation formulas are correct.

Note that with CPRI-A support, as ALU radios perform different representation of thermal noise power than Nokia radios, the RX gain of ALU radios corresponding to Nokia defined rxScalingFactor for CPRI case shall have some bias, which are very little for BW 15MHz and 20MHz and can be neglected, but for BW 5MHz and 10Mhz, the bias is big, so L1SW shall need to compensate it with the corrective terms for FDD only (Refer to [11377105: Power Scaling, CPRI-A](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ccPCEPviEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when “cpriDialectIndication == CPRI-A” of UlCell\_SetupReq from L3 CP-RT:In case of 5MHz, pCorChannelType is – 5 dB; in case of 10MHz, pCorChannelType is – 2 dB.

And these pCorChannelType parameters shall be applied to those power measurement reports, such as RSSI, noise power and rx power, etc. which are converted to dBm.

---

To account for the possibility that the formulas in the previous sub-sections, allowing the conversion of measurements to dBm before they are sent to 5G-L2-PS, are incorrect due to some gains being overlooked in the Rx processing chain, it is proposed, at least in the short term, to introduce additive corrective terms (in dB) in the previous power computation formulas. The assumptions with these corrective terms is that the previous formulas are wrong only due to the omission of a fixed gain. Assuming that this overlooked gain can be different for each physical signal or channel, a corrective term is proposed for each physical signal and channel. Note that it is not certain a priori that the corrective term should be the same for all power measurements performed on a particular physical signal or channel, but it is considered a reasonable assumption. It is hoped that measurements will be made soon that will allow to confirm this assumption.

The corrective terms would be determined by calibration (i.e., by comparing measured and trusted values of signal or noise powers with the values computed by L1-SW and by compensating any difference by corrective terms).

The corrective terms will be denoted pCorChannelType (pCorPusch, pCorPucch (F0/F1/F2/F3), pCorSrs and pCorPrach for PUSCH, PUCCH (F0/F1/F2/F3), SRS and PRACH, respectively) and will be expressed in dB.  The formulas including the corrective terms are of the type:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
$A\_{dBm} = 10 \cdot \log\_{10} A + \text{powerUnitChannelType}\_{dBm} + \text{pCorChannelType}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3160.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]    (equation 2.5.6.2-1)

and

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
$B\_{dBm} = 10 \cdot \log\_{10} B + \text{powerUnitChannelType}\_{dBm} + \text{pCorChannelType}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3160.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.6.2-2)

The default value for all pCorChannelType parameters will be 0, since the formulas in section [11419826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-epfvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) are believed to be correct, but this may evolve depending on the outcome of the calibrations.

The intention is that all there corrective terms are eventually removed once confirmation has been obtained through measurements that all power computation formulas are correct.

With CPRI-A support, as ALU radios perform different representation of thermal noise power than Nokia radios, the RX gain of ALU radios corresponding to Nokia defined rxScalingFactor for CPRI case shall have some bias, which are very little for BW 15MHz and 20MHz and can be neglected, but for BW 5MHz and 10Mhz, the bias is big, so L1SW shall need to compensate it with the corrective terms for FDD only (Refer to [11377105: Power Scaling, CPRI-A](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ccPCEPviEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when “cpriDialectIndication == CPRI-A” of UlCell\_SetupReq from L3 CP-RT:In case of 5MHz, pCorChannelType is – 5 dB; in case of 10MHz, pCorChannelType is – 2 dB.

Note: CPRI-A is only applicable to ABIO.

And these pCorChannelType parameters shall be applied to those power measurement reports, such as RSSI, noise power and rx power, etc. which are converted to dBm.

## 2.5.7 Rx power scaling formulas for Loner only

### 2.5.7.1 Rx power scaling formulas for PUSCH

**2.5.7.1.0-2**  (ID: `11420409`)

Rx power scaling formulas for PUSCH
11420409:
Rx power scaling formulas for PUSCH

Rx power scaling formulas for PUSCH

Rx power scaling formulas for PUSCH

11420409:

Rx power scaling formulas for PUSCH
The Rx power scaling formulas for PUSCH are implemented as follows. Calculation of power unit for PUSCH:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
`scalerPusch = 2^(3-ageShiftPusch) * alphaAgcPusch * xScale * 2^-(shift+Qiq-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]    (equation 2.5.7.1-1)

Where agcShiftPusch is calculated dynamically by FPGA based on 1st OFDM symbol of PUSCH, for the value it can refer section [11418920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-a_HPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), alphaAgcPusch is an extra coefficient depends on several parameters, detail can refer section [11418935](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-a_HvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), xScale = 0.5. Then

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
`scalerPusch_dB = 20 * log_10(scalerPusch)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.7.1-2)

For CPRI case

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue color against a white background. The formula is:
`powerUnitPusch_dBm = 0.1 * rxScalingFactor - 20 * log10(NFFT) - scalerPusch_dB`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]    (equation 2.5.7.1-3)

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light gray color against a white background. The formula is:
`powerUnitPusch_RTWPdBm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - 20 log10(NFFT) + 20 log10(2^IQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]     (equation 2.5.7.1-4)

For eCPRI case

[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`powerUnitPusch_dBm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - scalerPusch_dB`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]   (equation 2.5.7.1-5)

The [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "powerUnitPusch" followed by "dBm" in subscript. The text is in a light gray color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] shall be applied to PUSCH channel power metrics calculation of noise power, de-boost RSSI (both cumulated RSSI on all antennas and antenna wise RSSI  and received signal power (both cumulated rx power on all antennas and antenna wise rx power).

**[CB009794-F]**

Linear antenna wise RSSI (de-boost) and antenna wise noise (both normalized to 1 PRB) shall be reported in aW with unit of [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "10(-18)". The expression is written in a light gray color against a white background. The numbers and symbols are clear and legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6] W, so the calculation of power unit of these power metrics shall be

[image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
powerUnitPusch\_aw = 10^((powerUnitPusch\_dBm + pCorPusch) / 10) \* 10^15[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]      (equation 2.5.7.1-6)

In case of invalid measurement, antenna wise RSSI and antenna wise noise shall be set to [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "10^(-17)". The number 10 is written in a larger font, and the exponent -17 is written in a smaller font above and to the right of the 10, enclosed in parentheses.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8] W (10 aW).

**[End CB009794-F]**

The [image-9][image\_desc]powerUnitPusch\_RTWPdBm[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9] shall be applied to rtwpOfAnt calculation since RTWP is calculated by L1 FPGA before de-mapper without AGC scaling, etc.

The [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains the text "scaler Pusch" in a light blue, italicized font. The text is positioned at the bottom of the image against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3166.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10] shall be not used in the calculation of shortTermTaPeakAmp due to the meaning of shortTermTaPeakAmp (Amplitude of the highest power peak of the channel impulse response, actually it is neither an amplitude nor a power, but a SINR).

Please note that in case of no grant scheduled (numOfGrants = 0 in receive request), this ensures that RTWP measurements are executed in case of slots without PUSCH traffic, and RSSI will be filled with predefined value – 140 dBm in that case.

---

### 2.5.7.2 Rx power scaling formulas for SRS

**2.5.7.2.0-1**  (ID: `11420441`)

Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11420441:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
SRS measurements reported to L2PS are SNR (signal to noise ratio in dB on received unprecoded SRS), ulPmiRank1Sinr (Prediction of SINR in dB for PUSCH for given ulPmiRank1), ulPmiRank2Sinr (Prediction of SINR in dB for PUSCH for given ulPmiRank2) and shortTermTaPeakAmp (Amplitude of the highest power peak of the channel impulse response, actually it is neither an amplitude nor a power, but a SINR).

Then it is fine to calculate those parameters without rescaling the power scaling factors introduced and the results are not impacted.

With feature 5GC002244-A introduce, received power of each measured rx antenna stream need to be reported, so L1SW need to rescale the measurements before sending them to L2PS.

The Rx power scaling formulas for SRS are implemented as follows: Calculation of power unit for SRS:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light gray font on a white background. The formula is:
`scalerSrs = 2^(3-ageShiftSrs) * alphaAgcSrs * xScale * 2^-(shift+Q1Q-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3168.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]    (equation 2.5.7.2-1)

Where agcShiftSrs is calculated dynamically by FPGA based on 1st OFDM symbol of SRS and it is SRS comb specific, alphaAgcSrs =1, xScale = 0.5. Then

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font on a white background. The equation is:
`scalerSrs_dB = 20 · log₁₀(scalerSrs)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3168.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.7.2-1)

For CPRI case

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font on a white background. The equation is:
`powerUnitSrsdBm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - 20 log10(NFFT) - scalerSrSdB`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3168.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]    (equation 2.5.7.2-3)

For eCPRI case

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`powerUnitSrs_dBm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - scalerSrs_dB`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3168.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]    (equation 2.5.7.2-4)

The [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "powerUnitSrs\_dBm". The text is in a light blue color and is slightly blurry. The text is positioned at the bottom of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3168.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] shall be applied to SRS channel power metrics calculation of received signal power on each measured antenna stream.

The Rx power scaling formulas for PUCCH are implemented as follows. Calculation of power unit for PUCCH:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light gray font on a white background. The formula is:

`scaler Pucch_dB = 20 * log_10(scaler Pucch)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3170.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.7.3-2)

For CPRI case

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font on a white background. The equation is:
`powerUnitPucchasm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - 20 log10(NFFT) - scaler Pucchab`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3170.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]    (equation 2.5.7.3-3)

For eCPRI case

For long PUCCH F1, one additional normalization factor pNormF1 needs to add into [image-4][image\_desc]powerUnitPucch$\_{dBm}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3170.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] to normalize the PUCCH F1 power measurements (noise, rxPower and RSSI). The default value is -10.7 dB.

The [image-5][image\_desc]powerUnitPucch$\_{dBm}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3170.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] shall be applied to PUCCH channel power metrics calculation of noise power, RSSI, received signal power, the [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "scaler Pucch" in a light blue, italicized font. The text is centered horizontally and positioned towards the bottom of the image. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3170.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6] shall be not used in the calculation of shortTermTaPeakAmp due to the meaning of shortTermTaPeakAmp (Amplitude of the highest power peak of the channel impulse response, actually it is neither an amplitude nor a power, but a SINR).

The formula is: $$ \text{scalerPrach}(n) = \frac{\text{decimationFactor} \cdot 2^{-\frac{\text{max_shift}+\text{ant_shift}}{2}} \cdot 2^{-(\text{shift}+\text{Q} {\text{IQ}}-\text{in})}}{\text{postFftScalingFactor} \cdot \text{postIfftScalingFactor}} $$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3172.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]    (equation 2.5.7.4-1) This [image-1][image_desc]The image contains the text "scalerPrach(n)" in a light blue color against a white background. Calculation of scalerPusch (There is variant of *equation 2.5.5.2-1 for CPRI since inputGainPusch (as Spre) is already taken into use in the power calculation (linear value) including RSSI and noise power and RTWP by MDAB/DSP (Reference: [12698255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_9D-bEFyfEfCPFofqMEsORA) chapter 13.2.5.1.1), Spost = 1 so it is not visible in the* equation 2.5.5.2-1):**For CPRI case and OBSAI case:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`scalerPusch = 2^-(qIQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3179.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]    (equation 2.5.8.1-1)
For eCPRI case:
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`scalerPusch = 2^nshift * 2^-(QIQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3179.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.8.1-2)
Please refer section [11419907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-fQhPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the value of [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Q10-fm" in a blue, italicized font. The text is positioned at the bottom left of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3175.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2], refer section [11419208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-cNOvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the calculation of [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of text. The visible text appears to be "nShift". The letters are in a blue-grey color with a slight orange tint, and the background is white. The right edge of the image is bordered by a thick black line.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3175.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3], and the calculation is done for selective OFDM symbols where DMRS of any UE present** and data symbol, typical scenarios:\*\*
• DMRS of all UE are located at the first OFDM symbol, then only the first symbol will be scaled.
• DMRS of all UE are located at the same OFDM symbols, then those symbols having DMRS will be scaled independently.
• DMRS of different UE are located at different OFDM symbols, then those symbols having DMRS will be scaled independently.
• The first OFDM symbol having data will be scaled independently for data scaling only, or else the first OFDM symbol having DMRS will be scaled and reused for data scaling. Examples for data scaling as below:
[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a table with the header "Type A". The table has rows labeled "Estimation:" and "Scaling:", and columns labeled with numbers from 0 to 13.
The "Estimation:" row indicates that "DMRS" is present in columns 2-3 and 10-11. Below "DMRS", "data" is listed in column 0. "R1" is listed in column 3, and "R2" is listed in column 11.
The "Scaling:" row shows "D1" in columns 0-1, 4-10, and 12-13. "R1" is listed in column 3, and "R2" is listed in column 11.
The cells in columns 0-11 and 10-13 are highlighted in yellow, with a darker orange highlight in columns 2-3 and 10-11.

| **[CB012149-AB]** |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| • First time scaling for the first data symbol of non-switching UEs and second time scaling for the first data symbol of switching UEs. In both cases all allocated PRBs are included, so there is always only a single scaling per symbol and antenna. The data symbols before the second calculated data scaling are scaled with the first data scaling. The rest of the data symbols are scaled with the second data scaling. One example as below |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| FR1-FDD-CPRI | supported |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

### 2.5.8.2 Rx power scaling formulas for SRS

**2.5.8.2.0-2**  (ID: `11421337`)

Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
11421337:
Rx power scaling formulas for SRS
In LOKI the SRS measurements are performed in MDAB by L1SW, and the reported paramters to L2PS related to power measurements are SNR (signal to noise ratio in dB on received unprecoded SRS), ulPmiRank1Sinr (Prediction of SINR in dB for PUSCH for given ulPmiRank1), ulPmiRank2Sinr (Prediction of SINR in dB for PUSCH for given ulPmiRank2) and shortTermTaPeakAmp (Amplitude of the highest power peak of the channel impulse response, actually it is neither an amplitude nor a power, but a SINR).

Then it is fine to calculate those parameters without rescaling the power scaling factors introduced.

With feature 5GC001294-A introduce, received power of each measured rx antenna stream need to be reported, so L1SW need to rescale the measurements before sending them to L2PS.

The Rx power scaling formulas for SRS are implemented as follows:

Calculation of scalerSrs (There is variant of *equation 2.5.5.2-1 for CPRI since inputGainPusch (as Spre) is already taken into use in the power calculation (linear value) by MDAB/DSP (Reference: [12698255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_9D-bEFyfEfCPFofqMEsORA) chapter 2.7.3.3), Spost = 1 so it is not visible in the* equation 2.5.5.2-1):\*\*

For CPRI case and OBSAI case:

[image-0][image\_desc]scalerSrs = 2^-(Q\_IQ-in)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3182.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]    (equation 2.5.8.2-1)

For eCPRI case:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font against a white background. The equation is:
`scalerSrs = 2^nShift(r) * 2^-(Q_in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3182.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.8.2-2)

Please refer section [11419907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-fQhPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the value of [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Q10-fm" in a blue, italicized font. The text is positioned at the bottom left of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3175.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2], refer section [11419208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-cNOvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the calculation of [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of text. The visible text appears to be "nShift". The letters are in a blue-grey color with a slight orange tint, and the background is white. The right edge of the image is bordered by a thick black line.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3175.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3], and only sub-carriers on occupied comb and sub-band are used for [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of text. The visible text appears to be "nShift". The letters are in a blue-grey color with a slight orange tint, and the background is white. The right edge of the image is bordered by a thick black line.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3182.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] calculation, multiple UEs share same comb and sub-band resources will use the same scaling factor.

Then the dB value of [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of text. The visible text appears to be "scalerSrs". The letters are in a blue, italicized font. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3182.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]

[image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font on a white background. The equation is:
`scalerSrs_dB = 20 · log₁₀(scalerSrs)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3182.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]    (equation 2.5.8.2-3)

For CPRI case

[image-7][image\_desc]powerUnitSrs$*{dBm}$ = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - 10 log$*{10}$(N$*{FFT}$) - scalerSrs$*{dBm}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3182.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]    (equation 2.5.8.2-4)

For eCPRI case

[image-8][image\_desc]The image contains the following text: powerUnitSrs\_dBm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - scalerSrs\_dB[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3182.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8]    (equation 2.5.8.2-5)

Calculation of the received signal power on each Rx “physical” antenna port, normalized to 1 PRB, unit dBm:

[image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
`rxPower_per_Ant(dBm) = 10log10(rxPowerDSP-SRS-perAnt) + powerUnitSrsdBm + pCorSrs`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3182.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]    (equation 2.5.8.2-6)

Above requirement support based on technology and HW board as below table:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Technology** | **ABIO** | **ABIN** | **ASOE** | **ASOF** | **RINLINE1** |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI | supported | supported | supported | - | - |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | supported | supported | supported | **[CB009223-C] supported** [End CB009223-C]\*\*\*\* | - |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | - | - | - | supported |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | supported | - | supported | **[CB009223-D] supported** [End CB009223-D]\*\*\*\* | - |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | supported | supported | supported | supported |
| FR2-TDD-CPRI | - | - | - | - | - |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | - | - | - | - |

RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2.

Calculation of scalerPrach (i): (for the ith preamble in the slot)

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue font on a white background. The formula is:
`scalerPrach = 2^nShift * fdAgcGain * prchScalingFactor * 2^-(IQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]     (equation 2.5.8.4-4)

Please refer section [11419136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-cNN_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the detail calculation of [image-4][image\_desc]decimateScalingFactor[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3187.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4], refer section [11419031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-cNMfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the calculation of [image-5][image\_desc]prachtimeAgcGain[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3187.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5], refer section [11419049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-cNNPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the calculation of [image-6][image\_desc]prchScalingFactor[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3187.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6], refer section [11419907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-fQhPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the value of [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Q10-fm" in a blue, italicized font. The text is positioned at the bottom left of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3175.003.png[/image\_path][/image-7], refer section [11419208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-cNOvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the calculation of [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of text. The visible text appears to be "nShift". The letters are in a blue-grey color with a slight orange tint, and the background is white. The right edge of the image is bordered by a thick black line.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3175.004.png[/image\_path][/image-8], refer section [11419240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-cNPfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the calculation of [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains the text "fdAgcGain" in a light blue color against a white background. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9] and the calculation is based on each PRACH occasion.

First L1SW shall read noise\_power[i] and peak\_power[i] (dB value, note 1) (refer Table 18-12 PRCH Report format of Reference: [13349496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_creYYeqqEfCnwLcpJWh_Zw)) for the ith preamble from PRCH report, then the dB value of [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains the text "SNRdB" in a blurry, light blue font. The text is positioned in the bottom left corner of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10], [image-11][image\_desc]The image contains the text "noisePower" followed by "dB" in subscript. The text is in a light gray color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11] and [image-12][image\_desc]The image contains the text "peakPower" followed by "dB" in subscript. The text is in a light gray color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12] are calculated as

[image-13][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in light gray text on a white background. The formula is:
SNR$*{dB}$ = peak$*{power[i]}$ · dbScale - 30 - NpeBias$\_{dB}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.014.png[/image\_path][/image-13]    (equation 2.5.8.4-5)

[image-14][image\_desc]noisePower$*{dB}$ = noise\_power[i] · dbScale + NpeBias$*{dB}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.015.png[/image\_path][/image-14]    (equation 2.5.8.4-6)

[image-15][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
`peakPower_dB = peak_power[i] * dbScale - 30 + noise_power[i] * dbScale`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.016.png[/image\_path][/image-15]    (equation 2.5.8.4-7)

Where, [image-16][image\_desc]The image contains the text "dbScale" in a blurry, light blue font against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.017.png[/image\_path][/image-16] value depends on the DB\_CONV\_MODE field in PRACH\_JD\_SYS\_CFG\_S.

If DB\_CONV\_MODE is set to 0, then

[image-17][image\_desc]The image contains the text "dbScale = 0.1". The text is in a light gray color against a white background. The font appears to be a sans-serif font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.018.png[/image\_path][/image-17]    (equation 2.5.8.4-8)

Else if DB\_CONV\_MODE is set to 1, then

[image-18][image\_desc]The image contains the text "dbScale = 0.01". The text is in a light gray color against a white background. The font appears to be a sans-serif font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.019.png[/image\_path][/image-18]    (equation 2.5.8.4-9)

Due to LOKI NPE is underestimated, NPE bias values are obtained from simulation, and the values are dependent on the length of ZC sequence and number of combined antennas.

Table-1 gives NpeBiasdB values for long format with L\_RA = 839.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| NumCombinedAnt | 2 | 4 | 8 | 16 | 32 |
| NpeBiasdB | 0.95 | 0.73 | 0.59 | 0.49 | 0.39 |

Table-2 gives NpeBiasdB values for short format with L\_RA = 139.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| NumCombinedAnt | 2 | 4 | 6 | 8 | 12 | 16 | 24 | 32 | 48 | 96 |
| NpeBiasdB | 1.96 | 1.38 | 1.16 | 1.03 | 0.88 | 0.80 | 0.70 | 0.66 | 0.58 | 0.52 |

In LOKI, PRCH shall not tell which preamble is detected, so L1SW needs to detect this using predefined dtx threhold per 5gmax, the reader can refer chapter 3.4 for more detail. Then L1SW shall calculate the noise power (in unit dBm) and peak metirc (linear value) for the detected preambles and deliver the power reports to L2PS.

Calculation of noise power over the bandwidth occupied by PRACH (note 2), received on all Rx “physical” antennas and on all repetitions, unit dBm:

For CPRI case and OBSAI case:

[image-19][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
noisePower = $\frac{bandwidthRatio \cdot N\_{RX} \cdot cohCombLen}{scalerPrach} \cdot 10^{\frac{noisePower\_{dB}+0.1 \cdot rxScalingFactor+pCorPrach}{10}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.020.png[/image\_path][/image-19]    (equation 2.5.8.4-10)

For eCPRI case:

[image-20][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
noisePower = $\frac{L\_{RA} \cdot N\_{RX} \cdot cohCombLen}{scalerPrach} \cdot 10^{\frac{noisePower\_{dB} + 0.1 rxScalingFactor + pCorPrach}{10}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.021.png[/image\_path][/image-20]    (equation 2.5.8.4-11)

Then dBm value:

[image-21][image\_desc]noisePower\_dBm = 10 \* log10(noisePower)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.022.png[/image\_path][/image-21]    (equation 2.5.8.4-12)

Calculation of peak metric over the bandwidth occupied by PRACH (note 3), received on all Rx “physical” antennas in linear value:

For CPRI case and OBSAI case:

[image-22][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light gray font on a white background. The formula is:
peakMetric = (bandwidthRatio \* NRX) / (scalerPrach \* LRA) \* 10^((peakPowerdB + 0.1 \* rxScalingFactor + pCorPrach) / 10)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.023.png[/image\_path][/image-22]    (equation 2.5.8.4-13)

For eCPRI case:

[image-23][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
peakMetric = $\frac{N\_{RX}}{scalerPrach}$ $\cdot$ 10$^{\frac{peakPower\_{dB}+0.1 \cdot rxScalingFactor+pCorPrach}{10}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.024.png[/image\_path][/image-23]    (equation 2.5.8.4-14)

Where, PRACH band width ratio in equation 2.5.8.4-8 and equation 2.5.8.4-11 is calcuated with

[image-24][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue font on a white background. The formula is:
`bandwidthRatio = L_RA * prachScs / samplingRate`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3188.025.png[/image\_path][/image-24]     (equation 2.5.8.4-15)

**Note 1: The peak\_power reported by PRCH is actually SNR of peak energy samples on each preamble, so the final peak\_power needs to add noise\_power in dB.**

**Note 2: The noise power output from PRCH is averaged to one subcarrier**

**Note 3: The peak power output from PRCH is sum of all PRACH subcarriers.**

**Note 4: "PRCH" in above description refer to the MHAB "PRACH Preamble Detector" in Loki.**

Above requirement support based on technology and HW board as below table:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Technology** | **ABIO** | **ABIN** | **ASOE** | **ASOF** | **RINLINE1** |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI | supported | supported | supported | - | - |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | supported | supported | supported | **[CB009223-C] supported** [End CB009223-C]\*\*\*\* | - |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | - | - | - | supported |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | supported | - | supported | **[CB009223-D] supported** [End CB009223-D]\*\*\*\* | - |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | supported | supported | supported | supported |
| FR2-TDD-CPRI | - | - | - | - | - |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | - | - | - | - |

RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2.

Then the dB value of [image-8][image_desc]The image contains the text "scalerPusch" in a grey color. Calculation of noise power, rx power and RSSI per PRB, summed on all Rx “physical” antennas, for PUCCH format 0, unit dBm:

[image-12][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue font against a white background. The formula is:

### 2.5.9.4 Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH

#### 2.5.9.4.0-1 Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH 11422474: Rx Power scaling formulas for PRACH The Rx power scaling formulas for PRACH are implemented as follows: Calculation of scalerPrach (i): (for the ith preamble in the slot) For CPRI case and OBSAI case: [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light gray, italicized font against a white background. The formula is: scalerPrach = decimatescalingFactor · sqrt(N_IFFT) · fdAgcGain · prchscalingFactor · 2^-(Q_in) [/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]   (equation 2.5.9.4-1) For eCPRI case: [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is: scalerPrach = fdAgcGain · prchScalingFactor · 2^-(IQ-in) [/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]    (equation 2.5.9.4-2) Please refer section 11419439 for the detail calculation of [image-2][image_desc]decimateScalingFactor[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.003.png[/image_path][/image-2], refer section 11419312 for the value of [image-3][image_desc]The image contains the text "N IFFT" in a blue font. The text is slightly blurry.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.004.png[/image_path][/image-3], refer section 11419364 for the calculation of [image-4][image_desc]The image contains the text "fdAgcGain" in a light blue color against a white background. The text is slightly blurry.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.005.png[/image_path][/image-4], refer section 11419383 for the calculation of [image-5][image_desc]prchScalingFactor[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.006.png[/image_path][/image-5], refer section 11419451 for the calculation of [image-6][image_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of text. The right edge of the image is bordered by a thick black line.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3193.005.png[/image_path][/image-6], and the calculation is based on each PRACH occasion. First L1SW shall read noise_power[i] and peak_power[i] ( linear value)  for the ith preamble from PRCH report, then L1SW shall calculate the noise power (in unit dBm) and peak metric (linear value) for the detected preambles and deliver the power reports to L2PS Calculation of noise power over the bandwidth occupied by PRACH (note 1), received on all Rx “physical” antennas and on all repetitions, unit dBm: For CPRI case and OBSAI case: [image-7][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: noisePower = $\frac{\text{noise_power}[i] \cdot \text{bandWidthRatio} \cdot N_{RX} \cdot \text{cohCombLen}}{\text{scaler Prach}} \cdot 10^{\frac{0.1 \cdot \text{rxScalingFactor}+\text{pCorPrach}}{10}}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.008.png[/image_path][/image-7]  (equation 2.5.9.4-3) For eCPRI case: [image-8][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: noise Power = (noise_power[i] * L_RA * N_RX * CohCombLen) / scalerPrach * 10^((0.1 * rxScalingFactor + pCorPrach) / 10)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.009.png[/image_path][/image-8]    (equation 2.5.9.4-4) Then dBm value: [image-9][image_desc]noisePower_dBm = 10 * log10(noisePower)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.010.png[/image_path][/image-9]    (equation 2.5.9.4-5) Calculation of peak metric over the bandwidth occupied by PRACH (note 2), received on all Rx “physical” antennas in linear value: For CPRI case and OBSAI case: [image-10][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: peakMetric = (peak_power[i] * bandWidthRatio * NRX) / (scalerPrach * LRA) * 10^((0.1 * rxScalingFactor + pCorPrach) / 10)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.011.png[/image_path][/image-10]    (equation 2.5.9.4-6) For eCPRI case: [image-11][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: peakMetric = (peak_power[i] * NRX / scalerPrach) * 10(0.1 * rxScalingFactor + pCorPrach) / 10[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.012.png[/image_path][/image-11]    (equation 2.5.9.4-7) Where, PRACH band width ratio in equation 2.5.9.4-3 and equation 2.5.9.4-6 is calculated with [image-12][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light blue font on a white background. The formula is: bandwidthRatio = L_RA * prachScs / samplingRate [/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_3201.013.png[/image_path][/image-12]     (equation 2.5.9.4-8) Note 1: The noise power output from PRCH is averaged to one subcarrier Note 2: The peak power output from PRCH is sum of all PRACH subcarriers. Above requirement support based on technology as below table: | | | | --- | --- | | Technology | Thor | | FR1-FDD-OBSAI | supported | | FR1-FDD-CPRI | supported | | FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | | FR1-TDD-CPRI | supported | | FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | | FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | - | | FR2-TDD-CPRI | - | | FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | supported | (ID: 11422474)

• DMRS of all UE are located at the first OFDM symbol, then only the first symbol will be scaled.
• DMRS of all UE are located at the same OFDM symbols, then those symbols having DMRS will be scaled independently.
• DMRS of different UE are located at different OFDM symbols, then those symbols having DMRS will be scaled independently.
Only the nShift calculated from the first DMRS symbol shall be used for the calculation of power measurements since these measurements are based on only the first DMRS symbol.
Then the dB value of [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "scalerPusch" in a grey color. [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
`scalerPusch_dB = 20 * log_10(scalerPusch)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]    (equation 2.5.10.1-3)
[CB012115-SR-JA]

`scalerPusch_dB_RTWP = 20 * log_10 (scalerPusch_RTWP)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8]    (equation 2.5.10.1-4)
[End CB012115-SR-JA]
And to convert the final power report to dBm value,
[CB012115-SR-JA]
For CPRI case:
[image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
`powerUnitPuscharm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - 20 log10(NFFT) - Scaler Puschar`
The equation appears to be a formula related to power unit calculation, possibly in a telecommunications or signal processing context, given the terms like "Puscharm", "rxScalingFactor", "NFFT" (likely Fast Fourier Transform size), and "Scaler Puschar". The subscript "dB" is present on "Puscharm" and "Puschar", indicating decibels.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]    (equation 2.5.10.1-5)
[image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light gray font on a white background. The formula is:
`powerUnitPusch_dBm,RTWP = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - 20 log10(NFFT) - scalerPusch_dB,RTWP`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10]    (equation 2.5.10.1-6)
[End CB012115-SR-JA]
For eCPRI case:
[image-11][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`powerUnitPusch_dBm = 0.1 rxScalingFactor - scalerPusch_dB`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11]    (equation 2.5.10.1-7)
Calculation of noise power, sum of average power on all Rx “physical” antenna ports, normalized to 1 PRB, unit dBm:
[image-12][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
noisePower (dBm) = 10log10(noisePower(nonscaled)) + powerUnit Puschasm + pCorPusch[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12]    (equation 2.5.10.1-8)
Calculation of de-boosted RSSI on all Rx “physical” antenna ports, normalized to 1 PRB, unit dBm:
[image-13][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$RSSI\_{ant (nonScaled,de-boosted)} = \frac{RSSI\_{ant (nonScaled)} - noisePower\_{ant (nonScaled)}}{DMRS\_{BoostPUSCH}} + noisePower\_{ant (nonScaled)}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.014.png[/image\_path][/image-13]   (equation 2.5.10.1-9)
[image-14][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is presented on two lines.
The first line reads:
RSSI ant (de-boosted) (dBm)
The second line reads:
= 10log10(RSSI ant (nonScaled.de-boosted)) + powerUnitPuschdBm + pCorPusch
The equation appears to be defining or relating the "RSSI ant (de-boosted)" value in dBm to a logarithmic function of another RSSI value, along with two other terms: "powerUnitPuschdBm" and "pCorPusch". The subscripts and parenthetical notations suggest these are specific parameters or measurements within a technical context, likely related to signal strength or power in a communication system.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.015.png[/image\_path][/image-14](equation 2.5.10.1-10)
[image-15][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font on a white background. The equation is:
$RSSI\_{(nonScaled.de-boosted)} = \sum\_{ant=0}^{N\_{RX}-1} RSSI\_{ant (nonScaled.de-boosted)}$
The equation represents the RSSI (Received Signal Strength Indicator) for a non-scaled, de-boosted signal as the sum of the RSSI of individual antennas, from antenna 0 up to $N\_{RX}-1$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.016.png[/image\_path][/image-15]    (equation 2.5.10.1-11)
[image-16][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
RSSI$*{(de-boosted)}$ (dBm) = 10log10(RSSI$*{(nonScaled.de-boosted)}$) + powerUnit Pusch$*{dBm}$ + pCorPusch[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.017.png[/image\_path][/image-16]    (equation 2.5.10.1-12)
Calculation of the received signal power on all Rx “physical” antenna ports, normalized to 1 PRB, unit dBm:
[image-17][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$rxPower*{ant (nonScaled)} = \frac{RSSI\_{ant (nonScaled)} - noisePower\_{ant (nonScaled)}}{DMRS\_{BoostPUSCH}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.018.png[/image\_path][/image-17]    (equation 2.5.10.1-13)
[image-18][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
rxPower$*{ant}$ (dBm) = 10log10(rxPower$*{ant}$ (nonscaled)) + powerUnit$*{Pusch*{dBm}}$ + pCor$*{Pusch}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.019.png[/image\_path][/image-18]    (equation 2.5.10.1-14)
[image-19][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$rxPower*{(nonScaled)} = \frac{RSSI\_{(nonScaled)} - noisePower\_{(nonScaled)}}{DMRS\_{BoostPUSCH}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.020.png[/image\_path][/image-19]    (equation 2.5.10.1-15)
[image-20][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font on a white background. The equation is:
rxPower(dBm) = 10log10(rxPower(nonscaled)) + powerUnit Puschasm + pCorPusch[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.021.png[/image\_path][/image-20]    (equation 2.5.10.1-16)
Where [image-21][image\_desc]DMRS\_BoostPUSCH[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.022.png[/image\_path][/image-21] = 2 in case of number of DMRS CDM groups without data equal to 2, and [image-22][image\_desc]DMRS\_BoostPUSCH[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.022.png[/image\_path][/image-22] = 1 in case of number of DMRS CDM groups without data equal to 1.
[CB012115-SR-JA]
Calculation of RTWP on each Rx “physcial” antenna port, it is total wideband power, no need normalization, unit dBm:
[image-23][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
RTWPant (dBm) = 10log10(RTWPant (nonscaled)) + powerUnitPuschdBm.RTWP + pCorPusch[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.023.png[/image\_path][/image-23]    (equation 2.5.10.1-17)
Please note that in case of no grant scheduled (numOfGrants = 0 in receive request), this ensures that RTWP measurements are executed in case of slots without PUSCH traffic, RSSI will be filled with predefined value – 140 dBm.
[End CB012115-SR-JA]
[CB012115-SR-MF]
Linear antenna wise RSSI (de-boost) and antenna wise noise shall be reported in aW with unit of [image-24][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "10(-18)". The expression is written in a light gray color against a white background. The numbers and symbols are clear and legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.024.png[/image\_path][/image-24]W, so the calculation of power unit of these power metrics shall be
[image-25][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
`powerUnitPusch_aw = 10^(powerUnitPusch_dBm + pCorPusch)/10 * 10^15`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.025.png[/image\_path][/image-25]      (equation 2.5.10.1-18)
Calculation of de-boost antenna wise RSSI, normalized to 1 PRB, unit aW:
[image-26][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
$RSSI\_{ant(de-boost)}(aW) = RSSI\_{ant(nonScaled.de-boost)} \cdot powerUnitPusch\_{aw}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.026.png[/image\_path][/image-26]    (equation 2.5.10.1-19)
Calculation of antenna wise noise, normalized to 1 PRB, unit aW:
[image-27][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`noisePower_ant(aW) = noisePower_ant(nonScaled) * powerUnitPusch_aw`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.027.png[/image\_path][/image-27]     (equation 2.5.10.1-20)
In case of invalid measurement, antenna wise RSSI and antenna wise noise shall be set to [image-28][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "10^(-17)". The number 10 is written in a larger font, and the exponent -17 is written in a smaller font above and to the right of the 10, enclosed in parentheses.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3194.028.png[/image\_path][/image-28] W (10aW).
[End CB012115-SR-MF]

The Rx power scaling formulas for PRACH are implemented as follows:
Calculation of scalerPrach (i): (for the ith preamble in the slot)
**[CB012115-SR-JA]**
For CPRI case:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a light gray, italicized font against a white background. The formula is:
`scalerPrach = decimatescalingFactor · sqrt(N_IFFT) · fdAgcGain · prchscalingFactor · 2^-(Q_in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]   (equation 2.5.10.4-1)
Please refer section [12580939](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_c1uWUDIrEfCfjdcwDn2YOQ) for the detail calculation of [image-1][image\_desc]decimateScalingFactor[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.003.png[/image\_path][/image-1], refer section [12580739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_a3LHIDH4EfCfjdcwDn2YOQ) for the value of [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N IFFT" in a blue font. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.004.png[/image\_path][/image-2].
**[End CB012115-SR-JA]**
For eCPRI case:
[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
`scalerPrach = fdAgcGain · prchScalingFactor · 2^-(IQ-in)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.002.png[/image\_path][/image-3]    (equation 2.5.10.4-2)
Please refer section [12580738](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YdTFsDH4EfCfjdcwDn2YOQ) for the calculation of [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "fdAgcGain" in a light blue color against a white background. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4], refer section [12580741](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_d3HYIjH6EfCfjdcwDn2YOQ) for the calculation of [image-5][image\_desc]prchScalingFactor[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5], refer section [12580760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MKrR8TICEfCfjdcwDn2YOQ) for the value of [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Q10-fm" in a blue, italicized font. The text is positioned at the bottom left of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6], and the calculation is based on each PRACH occasion.
First L1SW shall read noise\_power[i] and peak\_power[i] (**linear value)  for the ith preamble from PRCH report, then L1SW shall calculate the noise power (in unit dBm) and peak metirc (linear value) for the detected preambles and deliver the power reports to L2PS**
Calculation of noise power over the bandwidth occupied by PRACH (note 1), received on all Rx “physical” antennas and on all repetitions, unit dBm:
**[CB012115-SR-JA]**
For CPRI case:
[image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
noisePower = $\frac{\text{noise\_power}[i] \cdot \text{bandWidthRatio} \cdot N\_{RX} \cdot \text{cohCombLen}}{\text{scaler Prach}} \cdot 10^{\frac{0.1 \cdot \text{rxScalingFactor}+\text{pCorPrach}}{10}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]  (equation 2.5.10.4-3)
**[End CB012115-SR-JA]**
For eCPRI case:
[image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
noise Power = (noise\_power[i] \* L\_RA \* N\_RX \* CohCombLen) / scalerPrach \* 10^((0.1 \* rxScalingFactor + pCorPrach) / 10)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8]    (equation 2.5.10.4-4)
Then dBm value:
[image-9][image\_desc]noisePower\_dBm = 10 \* log10(noisePower)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]    (equation 2.5.10.4-5)
 
 
Calculation of peak metric over the bandwidth occupied by PRACH (note 2), received on all Rx “physical” antennas in linear value:
**[CB012115-SR-JA]**
For CPRI case:
[image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
peakMetric = (peak\_power[i] \* bandWidthRatio \* NRX) / (scalerPrach \* LRA) \* 10^((0.1 \* rxScalingFactor + pCorPrach) / 10)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10]    (equation 2.5.9.10-6)
**[End CB012115-SR-JA]**
For eCPRI case:
[image-11][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
peakMetric = (peak\_power[i] \* NRX / scalerPrach) \* 10(0.1 \* rxScalingFactor + pCorPrach) / 10[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3201.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11]    (equation 2.5.10.4-7)
**Note 1: The noise power output from PRCH is averaged to one subcarrier**
**Note 2: The peak power output from PRCH is sum of all PRACH subcarriers.**
The supported channel and signal based on technology as below table:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Technology** | **Odin BB** | **Odin RU** | **UL channels & Signals** |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | **[CB012115-SR-JA] supported** [End CB012115-SR-JA]\*\*\*\* | - | PRACH |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | **[CB012115-SR-LA] supported** [End CB012115-SR-LA]\*\*\*\* | - | PRACH |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | **[CB012115-SR-IA] supported** [End CB012115-SR-IA]\*\*\*\* | - | PRACH |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | **[CB012115-SR-GA] supported** [End CB012115-SR-GA]\*\*\*\* | - | PRACH |

The right edge of the image is bordered by a thick black line.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3193.005.png[/image\_path][/image-8], and the calculation is done for selective OFDM symbols where DMRS of any UE present, typical scenarios:*****\****\*

• DMRS of all UE are located at the first OFDM symbol, then only the first symbol will be scaled.

• DMRS of all UE are located at the same OFDM symbols, then those symbols having DMRS will be scaled independently.

• DMRS of different UE are located at different OFDM symbols, then those symbols having DMRS will be scaled independently.

Only the nShift calculated from the first DMRS symbol shall be used for the calculation of power measurements since these measurements are based on only the first DMRS symbol.

**[End CB010708-I-UPD003]**

[image-13][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
$RSSI\_{ant (nonScaled,de-boosted)} = \frac{RSSI\_{ant (nonScaled)} - noisePower\_{ant (nonScaled)}}{DMRS\_{BoostPUSCH}} + noisePower\_{ant (nonScaled)}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3229.014.png[/image\_path][/image-13]   (equation 2.5.11.1.1-5)

RSSI$*{ant}$ (de-boosted) (dBm)
The second line reads:
= 10log10(RSSI$*{ant}$ (nonScaled.de-boosted)) + powerUnitPusch$\_{dBm}$ + pCorPusch[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3229.015.png[/image\_path][/image-14](equation 2.5.11.1.1-6)

$RSSI\_{(nonScaled.de-boosted)} = \sum\_{ant=0}^{N\_{RX}-1} RSSI\_{ant (nonScaled.de-boosted)}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3229.016.png[/image\_path][/image-15]    (equation 2.5.11.1.1-7)

RSSI(de-boosted) (dBm) = 10log10(RSSI(nonScaled.de-boosted)) + powerUnit Pusch\_dBm + pCorPusch
The formula appears to be related to signal strength measurements, possibly in a telecommunications context, given the terms "RSSI" (Received Signal Strength Indicator), "dBm" (decibels relative to one milliwatt), and "Pusch" (Physical Uplink Shared Channel). The formula calculates the de-boosted RSSI in dBm by taking the base-10 logarithm of the non-scaled de-boosted RSSI, and then adding two correction terms: "powerUnit Pusch\_dBm" and "pCorPusch".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_3229.017.png[/image\_path][/image-16]    (equation 2.5.11.1.1-8)
